#Nuxeo Training - NXQL, Search forms, content views
###What we want to do ####At the end of the course: - The tab content of BookLibrary with specific columns: Title, ISBN, Author, Creation date - A custom filter to filter through custom metadata - A custom advanced search form
###NXQL - Nuxeo Query Language Example: `SELECT * FROM Book WHERE bk:isbn ILIKE '%12%'`
returns documents of type Book or derived from Book having bk:isbn contains 12
- Query language  - Search documents  - Similar to SQL  - Only SELECT (no update or delete) - System fields: `ecm:primaryType`, `ecm:currentLifeCycleSate` - Document metadata: `schema_prefix:property_name` ####Tip: test NXQL Query Advanced search as an administrator ####Full documentation http://doc.nuxeo.com/display/NXDOC/NXQL
###NXQL Examples 

SELECT * FROM Document WHERE ecm:mixinType = 'Versionable' AND ecm:mixinType <> 'Downloadable'

SELECT * FROM Document WHERE ecm:parentId = '5442fff5-06f1-47c9-ac59-1e10ef8e985b'

SELECT * FROM Document WHERE dc:coverage STARTSWITH 'foo/bar'

SELECT * FROM Document WHERE dc:title = 'hello world 1' ORDER BY ecm:currentLifeCycleState

SELECT * FROM Document WHERE ecm:fulltext = 'world'
###Content View

Any list of documents that is the result of a specific query

####Used in many places in Nuxeo: - for the content of a folderish node - for the trash folder - for advanced search - for simple search - for faceted search - for virtual navigation - for custom business content listing on some projects
###Content View definition
  • WHERE clause of an NXQL query 
    ecm:mixinType != 'HiddenInNavigation' AND ecm:isCheckedInVersion = 0 AND ecm:currentLifeCycleState != 'deleted' and ecm:parentId= ?
  • Dynamical parameters (see the «?»)
    and a form layout to get the values for those parameters
  • A Result layout
    the definition of the columns displayed for the result
  • The list of additional columns
    that can be selected by the user to be added in the result layout
  • Default sort criteria, pagination options, UI options, ...

### Query Filter - Uses Where clause of NXQL - Can be parameterized - JbossEL access to Seam bean - `#{currentDocument.id}` - `#{currentDocument.path}` - `#{currentDocument.schema.property}` - `#{currentUser.name}` - Replace with `?` In the QueryFilter
###Filter form - Customize filter criteria - Document metadata  - Document properties (lifecycle state, path, etc.)  - Custom UI field  - Custom operators (STARTSWITH, EQUALS, etc.)
###Content tab - A content view - Defined per document type. - With the query 
select * From Document Where ecm:mixinType != 'HiddenInNavigation' AND ecm:isCheckedInVersion = 0 AND ecm:currentLifeCycleState != 'deleted' and ecm:parentId= ?
- `#{currentDocument.id}` for the dynamic parameter `?`
Defines the NXQL query as well as the columns to display (Result layout). On the same type, ability to add as many tabs as required, just by giving a content view definition.
###Result layout - Defines the result columns - Display fields with layout widgets - Ready to use widget types - Reusable: `Table Layout` (Listings & Views > Table Layouts)
###Table layout in Studio ![Table layout in Studio](img/contentview-tablelayout.png)

###Custom Advanced Search Form - Replace the default « Advanced Search » page - Can be setup in Domain/Workspace local configuration
In Nuxeo DM, using the Local configuration service, you can choose to display different advanced search screens depending on in which domain or workspace you are (see Manage tab > Local configuration). In studio, in Search And Listing > Advanced search, you can contribute the main advanced search screen. If you want to contribute other ones to use them in DM, you just need to contribute new content view and flag them with «advanced search», in the Studio interface. They will appear then in the Local Configuration.
